a"><div class=3D"nsiojc-0 cHvPUI"></div></div></div></div></div><div class=
=3D"WidthWrapper__ReadWidthWrapper-ccd-component-library__sc-1m6qjgq-3 exlk=
na"><section class=3D"sc-11f48jc-0 jDXwsl"><p class=3D"sc-a1mtb-0 jNMONS">G=
eneral Authority Seventies are Church leaders called by the <a href=3D"http=
s://www.churchofjesuschrist.org/learn/first-presidency">First Presidency</a=
> to be =E2=80=9Cespecial<sup>[1]</sup> witnesses=E2=80=9D and to assist th=
e Twelve in =E2=80=9Cbuilding up the church and regulating all the affairs=
=E2=80=9D and =E2=80=9Cpreaching and administering the gospel=E2=80=9D thro=
ughout the world (<a href=3D"http://www.churchofjesuschrist.org/study/scrip=
tures/dc-testament/dc/107.html?verse=3D25,34,38#p25">Doctrine and Covenants=
 107:25, 34, 38</a>). They act under the keys and direction of the <a href=
=3D"https://www.churchofjesuschrist.org/learn/quorum-of-the-twelve-apostles=
">Quorum of the Twelve Apostles</a>. In a revelation to Joseph Smith, the L=
ord taught, =E2=80=9CIt is the duty of the [Twelve Apostles] to call upon t=
he Seventy, when they need assistance, to fill the several calls for preach=
ing and administering the gospel=E2=80=9D (<a href=3D"https://www.churchofj=
esuschrist.org/study/scriptures/dc-testament/dc/107.html?verse=3D38#p38">Do=
ctrine and Covenants 107:38</a>).</p><p class=3D"sc-a1mtb-0 jNMONS">General=
 Authority Seventies serve full-time in the Church. They are generally rele=
ased in the year they turn 70 years old and are granted emeritus status. Li=
ke the Quorum of the Twelve, they travel widely to teach the gospel of Jesu=
s Christ, to support and counsel with Church leaders, and to assist in dire=
cting missionary work, humanitarian aid, temple building, family history, a=
nd other Church efforts. Some General Authority Seventies serve in the <a h=
ref=3D"https://www.churchofjesuschrist.org/learn/presidency-of-the-seventy"=
>Presidency of the Seventy</a>; others serve in <a href=3D"https://www.chur=
chofjesuschrist.org/learn/area-presidencies">Area Presidencies</a>. Many Se=
venties live near Church headquarters and assist in directing important Chu=
rch efforts from there.</p><p class=3D"sc-a1mtb-0 jNMONS">Though all Sevent=
ies have equal authority, some are designated as General Authorities and ot=
hers are designated as <a href=3D"https://www.churchofjesuschrist.org/learn=
/area-seventies">Area Seventies</a>.</p></section></div><div class=3D"Width=
